## לֹא דְבָר (id: 003492000000000)

לֹא דְבָר
=========

לֹא דְבָר (H1688b · H3810) — לִדְבִר, לֹו דְבָר

name · לֹא · דָּבָר

Names of Locations

Lodebar \= town; ► located east of the Jordan river in Gilead; assigned to tribe of Gad

[JOS 13:26](https://ref.ly/Josh13:26)1 · [2SA 9:4](https://ref.ly/2Sam9:4) · [2SA 9:5](https://ref.ly/2Sam9:5) · [2SA 17:27](https://ref.ly/2Sam17:27) · [AMO 6:13](https://ref.ly/Amos6:13)2

1 JOS 13:26 MT לִדְבִר LXX Δαβιρ \| RSV NIV NRSV "Debir" NJPS "Lidbir" \| HOTTP\-C לִדְבֹר (though agreeing that the text actually refers to Lodebar) CEV "Lidebor" \| NJB REB GNT "Lodebar" 2 AMO 6:13 RSV NIV NJPS NJB NRSV GNT CEV \| HOTTP\-A REB "nothing"

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Joshua 13:26; 2 Samuel 9:4; 2 Samuel 9:5; 2 Samuel 17:27; Amos 6:13

## לאה (id: 003495000000000)

לאה
===

לאה (H3811)

verb · תְּלָאָה

Weak

to wear oneself out \= action by which humans spend all their forces on a certain activity

[JER 9:4](https://ref.ly/Jer9:4)

Weak

to wear (someone) out \= causative process by which humans are caused to spend all their forces on a certain activity

[JER 12:5](https://ref.ly/Jer12:5)

Dry

to languish, to wither literally: to grow weary; \= state in which land has suffered from a period of drought ► as a result of which it can no longer bear fruit

[PSA 68:10](https://ref.ly/Ps68:10)

Unable

to be no longer able literally: to grow weary (doing something); hence: \= state in which humans and deities are no longer able to perform a certain event

[GEN 19:11](https://ref.ly/Gen19:11) · [EXO 7:18](https://ref.ly/Exod7:18) · [PRO 26:15](https://ref.ly/Prov26:15) · [ISA 1:14](https://ref.ly/Isa1:14) · [ISA 16:12](https://ref.ly/Isa16:12) · [ISA 47:13](https://ref.ly/Isa47:13) · [JER 6:11](https://ref.ly/Jer6:11) · [JER 15:6](https://ref.ly/Jer15:6) · [JER 20:9](https://ref.ly/Jer20:9)

Grieve

to be upset literally: to grow weary; hence: \= process by which humans feel upset

[JOB 4:2](https://ref.ly/Job4:2) · [JOB 4:5](https://ref.ly/Job4:5)

Grieve

to frustrate literally: to make weary; hence: \= process by which humans, deities, or circumstances cause (other) humans or deities to feel upset

[JOB 16:7](https://ref.ly/Job16:7) · [ISA 7:13](https://ref.ly/Isa7:13) · [ISA 7:13](https://ref.ly/Isa7:13) · [EZK 24:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek24:12) · [MIC 6:3](https://ref.ly/Mic6:3)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Jeremiah 9:4; Jeremiah 12:5; Psalms 68:10; Genesis 19:11; Exodus 7:18; Proverbs 26:15; Isaiah 1:14; Isaiah 16:12; Isaiah 47:13; Jeremiah 6:11; Jeremiah 15:6; Jeremiah 20:9; Job 4:2; Job 4:5; Job 16:7; Isaiah 7:13; Ezekiel 24:12; Micah 6:3

Wise

Spatial Referents

middle literally: heart; hence: \= a referent to the space right in the middle of something else, such as the sea, the heavens, or a tree

Names of Groups

**Collocation:** לֵב קָמָי

Leb\-Kamai, Chaldeans \= cryptic name for Chaldeans

[JER 51:1](https://ref.ly/Jer51:1)2

1 1SA 25:37 RSV NRSV NJB "his heart died" \| NIV "his heart failed" \| REB "he had a seizure" CEV "he had a heart attack" GNT "he suffered a stroke" \[1a] \| NJPS "courage died" \[1b] 2 JER 51:1 This is a so\-called atbash cipher, by which the aleph is encoded as a taw, the beth as a sin/shin, the gimel as a resh, etc.

Enio R. Mueller

## לִבְאָה (id: 003501000000000)

לִבְאָה
=======

לִבְאָה (H3833b) — לְבָאָה, לְבִיָּא

noun f · לָבִיא

Wild Animals

lioness \= female of the largest of the great cats, often being about 2\.8 meters from nose to tip of tail, standing as high as 1 meter (3 feet 3 inches) at the shoulder; pale yellowish brown in color; around the neck and shoulders of adult males grows a mane that is darker than the rest of their fur; ◄ Panthera leo; ► unclean animal; ≈ associated with aggression, fearlessness, and respect

[EZK 19:2](https://ref.ly/Ezek19:2) · [NAM 2:13](https://ref.ly/Nah2:13)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Ezekiel 19:2; Nahum 2:13


## לְבָאֹות (id: 003502000000000)

לְבָאֹות
========

לְבָאֹות (H3822)

name

Names of Locations

Lebaoth \= town, also referred to as Beth\-Lebaoth; ◄ territory of Simeon

[JOS 15:32](https://ref.ly/Josh15:32)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Joshua 15:32


## לבב (id: 003503000000000)

לבב
===

לבב (H3823)

verb · לֵב · לֵבָב · לְבִבָה · לִבָּה

Think

to get sense, to gain understanding literally: to get heart; hence: \= process by which humans learn to think for themselves as opposed to being easily swayed by what others say or do

[JOB 11:12](https://ref.ly/Job11:12)

Love

to capture (someone's) heart \= causative process by which humans inspire feelings of affection in someone else

[SNG 4:9](https://ref.ly/Song4:9) · [SNG 4:9](https://ref.ly/Song4:9)

Exist

to prepare cakes, to prepare dumplings \= causative action by which someone prepares heart\-shaped cakes or dumplings

[2SA 13:6](https://ref.ly/2Sam13:6) · [2SA 13:8](https://ref.ly/2Sam13:8)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Job 11:12; Song of Songs 4:9; 2 Samuel 13:6; 2 Samuel 13:8


## לְבַב (id: 003504000000000)

לְבַב
=====

לְבַב (A3825)

noun m

Think

heart, mind, attention, courage literally: heart; hence: \= the seat of knowledge, human reasoning, planning, intelligence, skill, affection and hatred, desire and satisfaction, humility and pride, courage and fear, joy and grief

[DAN 2:30](https://ref.ly/Dan2:30) · [DAN 4:13](https://ref.ly/Dan4:13) · [DAN 4:13](https://ref.ly/Dan4:13) · [DAN 5:20](https://ref.ly/Dan5:20) · [DAN 5:21](https://ref.ly/Dan5:21) · [DAN 5:22](https://ref.ly/Dan5:22) · [DAN 7:4](https://ref.ly/Dan7:4)

* **Associated Passages:** Daniel 2:30; Daniel 4:13; Daniel 5:20; Daniel 5:21; Daniel 5:22; Daniel 7:4


## לֵבָב (id: 003505000000000)

לֵבָב
=====

לֵבָב (H3824)

noun m · לֵב · לבב

People

heart \= the organ located in the centre of the human body that pumps the blood through our circulatory system, ≈ seen as the seat of knowledge, human reasoning, planning, intelligence, skill, affection and hatred, desire and satisfaction, humility and pride, courage and fear, joy and grief

[JDG 19:8](https://ref.ly/Judg19:8) · [NAM 2:8](https://ref.ly/Nah2:8)

(heart\-shaped) bread, (heart\-shaped) cake \= type of bread, possibly in the shape of a heart

## לְבֹונָה (id: 003509000000000)

לְבֹונָה
========

לְבֹונָה (H3828 · H3829) — לְבֹנָה

noun f

Spices

frankincense \= yellow or reddish gum produced by the Boswellia tree, a shrub that reaches 3 m high, with multiple trunks and small greenish or white flowers; the gum comes out in drops from the branches; ◄ Boswellia sacra; ► ingredient of the incense burned in the tabernacle

## לָבִיא (id: 003512000000000)

לָבִיא
======

לָבִיא (H3833a · H3833c) — לֶבֶא, לָבָא

noun m · לִבְאָה

Wild Animals

lion \= the largest of the great cats, often being about 2\.8 meters from nose to tip of tail, standing as high as 1 meter (3 feet 3 inches) at the shoulder; pale yellowish brown in color; around the neck and shoulders of adult males grows a mane that is darker than the rest of their fur; ◄ Panthera leo; ► unclean animal; ≈ associated with aggression, fearlessness, and respect

## לבן (id: 003513000000000)

לבן
===

לבן (H3835)

verb · לָבָן · לְבָנָה · לִבְנֶה · לָבָן · לִבְנָה · לְבָנֹון · לִבְנִי · לְבָנָה

Color

to become white literally: to become white; hence: \= process by which branches become light in color because they are stripped of their bark

[JOL 1:7](https://ref.ly/Joel1:7)

Innocent

to become pure literally: to become white; hence: \= causative process by which humans are considered free of guilt again, after having fallen into sin

[PSA 51:9](https://ref.ly/Ps51:9) · [DAN 11:35](https://ref.ly/Dan11:35) · [DAN 12:10](https://ref.ly/Dan12:10)

Right

**Collocation:** חֵטְא לבן

sins are made right literally: sins become white; hence: \= causative process by which the guilt resulting from wrongdoing will be removed

[ISA 1:18](https://ref.ly/Isa1:18)

verb · לְבֵנָה · מַלְבֵּן

Exist

to make bricks \= causative action by which humans produce bricks for building

[GEN 11:3](https://ref.ly/Gen11:3) · [EXO 5:7](https://ref.ly/Exod5:7) · [EXO 5:14](https://ref.ly/Exod5:14)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Joel 1:7; Psalms 51:9; Daniel 11:35; Daniel 12:10; Isaiah 1:18; Genesis 11:3; Exodus 5:7; Exodus 5:14

לבשׁ
====

לבשׁ (H3847 · A3848) — לָבוּשׁ

verb · לְבוּשׁ · מַלְבּוּשׁ · תִּלְבֹּשֶׁת

Dress

dressed, arrayed \= state in which humans wear certain clothes, often for a specific purpose

[1KI 22:10](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:10) · [2CH 5:12](https://ref.ly/2Chr5:12) · [2CH 18:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr18:9) · [EZR 3:10](https://ref.ly/Ezra3:10) · [PRO 31:21](https://ref.ly/Prov31:21) · [EZK 9:2](https://ref.ly/Ezek9:2) · [EZK 9:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek9:3) · [EZK 9:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek9:11) · [EZK 10:2](https://ref.ly/Ezek10:2) · [EZK 10:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek10:6) · [EZK 10:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek10:7) · [EZK 23:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek23:6) · [EZK 23:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek23:12) · [EZK 38:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek38:4) · [DAN 10:5](https://ref.ly/Dan10:5) · [DAN 12:6](https://ref.ly/Dan12:6) · [DAN 12:7](https://ref.ly/Dan12:7) · [ZEC 3:3](https://ref.ly/Zech3:3)

Dress

to put on (oneself), to wear \= action by which humans put on clothes or ornaments

Dress

to put on (someone else), to clothe \= causative action by which humans help other humans to put on clothes

Control

Cover

Cover

לְחִי

לְחִי (H3895 · H3896)

noun m

jaw, jawbone, cheek \= the lower bony structure of the skull of humans and certain animals that forms the framework of the mouth and holds the teeth

## לחך (id: 003567000000000)

לחך
===

לחך (H3897)

verb

Ingest

to lick up \= action by which animals ingest food with the help of their tongue

[NUM 22:4](https://ref.ly/Num22:4)

Insignificant

**Collocation:** לחך עָפָר

to lick the dust literally: to lick the dust; hence: \= process by which humans are deeply humiliated by being forced to lie prostrate on the ground before those in authority, and, in some cases, having to lick the dust from their feet

[PSA 72:9](https://ref.ly/Ps72:9) · [ISA 49:23](https://ref.ly/Isa49:23) · [MIC 7:17](https://ref.ly/Mic7:17)

Non\-Exist

to lick up \> to consume literally: to lick up; hence: \= a process by which humans completely use up all vegetation in a certain area

[NUM 22:4](https://ref.ly/Num22:4)

Non\-Exist

to lick up \> to consume literally: to lick up; hence: \= process by which liquids are completely vaporized by fire

[1KI 18:38](https://ref.ly/1Kgs18:38)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 22:4; Psalms 72:9; Isaiah 49:23; Micah 7:17; 1 Kings 18:38


## לחם (id: 003568000000000)

לחם
===

לחם (H3898)

verb · לָחֶם · לֶחֶם · מִלְחָמָה

Ingest

to eat \= action by which humans ingest food

[PSA 141:4](https://ref.ly/Ps141:4) · [PRO 4:17](https://ref.ly/Prov4:17) · [PRO 9:5](https://ref.ly/Prov9:5) · [PRO 23:6](https://ref.ly/Prov23:6)

Ingest

to have a meal \= action by which humans share a meal with other humans

[PRO 23:1](https://ref.ly/Prov23:1)

Dead

to be devoured literally: to be eaten; hence: \= process by which humans die as a result of hunger and sickness

[DEU 32:24](https://ref.ly/Deut32:24)

verb · לָחֶם · מִלְחָמָה

Conflict

to attack \= action by which humans or deities initiate a confrontation with (other) humans

## לֶחֶם (id: 003570000000000)

לֶחֶם
=====

לֶחֶם (H3899)

noun c · לחם · יָשֻׁבִי לֶחֶם

Bread · Food

bread, food \= a staple food ◄ made from a dough of water and either wheat or barley then baked; ► together with water considered the very basis of life, often used to refer to food in general

## לָחֶם (id: 003571000000000)

לָחֶם
=====

לָחֶם (H3901)

noun m · לחם

Conflict

fighter, fighting exact meaning unsure; probably: \= action by which humans engage in a confrontation with other humans; alternatively: \= a person engaged in a confrontation with other humans

[JDG 5:8](https://ref.ly/Judg5:8)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Judges 5:8

## לחץ (id: 003575000000000)

לחץ
===

לחץ (H3905)

verb · לַחַץ

Impact

to press oneself, to squeeze oneself \= action by which someone presses oneself against another object

[NUM 22:25](https://ref.ly/Num22:25)

Impact

to press, to hold (something) against (someone) \= action by which someone presses one object against another object

[NUM 22:25](https://ref.ly/Num22:25) · [2KI 6:32](https://ref.ly/2Kgs6:32)

Move

to press back, to drive back \= to force a large group of people back from their place of habitation into a smaller area

[JDG 1:34](https://ref.ly/Judg1:34)

Unsafe

to oppress, to afflict, oppression, affliction \= causative action by which humans cause hardship to other humans

[EXO 3:9](https://ref.ly/Exod3:9) · [EXO 22:20](https://ref.ly/Exod22:20) · [EXO 23:9](https://ref.ly/Exod23:9) · [JDG 2:18](https://ref.ly/Judg2:18) · [JDG 4:3](https://ref.ly/Judg4:3) · [JDG 6:9](https://ref.ly/Judg6:9) · [JDG 10:12](https://ref.ly/Judg10:12) · [1SA 10:18](https://ref.ly/1Sam10:18) · [2KI 13:4](https://ref.ly/2Kgs13:4) · [2KI 13:22](https://ref.ly/2Kgs13:22) · [PSA 56:2](https://ref.ly/Ps56:2) · [PSA 106:42](https://ref.ly/Ps106:42) · [ISA 19:20](https://ref.ly/Isa19:20) · [JER 30:20](https://ref.ly/Jer30:20) · [AMO 6:14](https://ref.ly/Amos6:14)

Reinier de Blois

## לחשׁ (id: 003577000000000)

לחשׁ
====

לחשׁ (H3907)

verb · לַחַשׁ

Speak

to whisper together \= action by which people talk softly among themselves to keep others from overhearing

[2SA 12:19](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:19) · [PSA 41:8](https://ref.ly/Ps41:8)

Control

charmer literally: whisperer; hence: \= person who (appear to) control a snake by means of sounds

[PSA 58:6](https://ref.ly/Ps58:6)

Reinier de Blois

## לְטָאָה (id: 003581000000000)

לְטָאָה
=======

לְטָאָה (H3911)

noun f

Small Animals

lacertid lizard \= relatively small type of lizard, with a length of about 15–20 cm; has a shiny, smooth, and colored skin; it feeds on insects and is found in orchards and woods;◄ \|iLacerta trilineata\|i\*; ► unclean animal and therefore not to be eaten

[LEV 11:30](https://ref.ly/Lev11:30)

Small Animals

agama lizard \= relatively large type of lizard, with a length of about 50–60 cm; of a dull gray color, except for the mating season, when the male develops bright colors; its tail is long and stiff and is raised when it runs; it is know for bobbing its head and doing "push\-ups" with its front legs; feeds on insects and smaller lizards; ◄ \|iagama stellio\|i\*, found in houses and on walls and rocks; ► unclean animal1

[LEV 11:30](https://ref.ly/Lev11:30)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Leviticus 11:30

## לִילִית (id: 003587000000000)

לִילִית
=======

לִילִית (H3917)

noun f

Birds

tawny owl, scops owl exact meaning unknown; possibly another name for the tawny owl, or: \= type of owl with tiny ears that is a mottled gray in color; by day it perches close to the trunk of a tree, where its mottled coloring blends in with the tree bark, making the owl look like the stump of a broken branch; it has a soft, trilled call; ≈ associated with demons

[ISA 34:14](https://ref.ly/Isa34:14)1

1 ISA 34:14 RSV "night hag" \| NIV "night creature" \| NJPS "the lilith" \| NJB NRSV "Lilith" \| REB "nightjar"

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 34:14

## למד (id: 003597000000000)

למד
===

למד (H3925)

verb · לִמּוּד · מַלְמָד · תַּלְמִיד

Know

learn \= process by which humans or animals acquire knowledge or skill from an identified or unidentified source, ► which usually results in a specific behavior or skill

Know

to teach, to instruct, to train \= causative action by which humans or deities cause humans or animals \-\- intentionally or unintentionally \-\- to acquire knowledge, skill, or behavior; usually refers to learning to the point of doing

## לָמָּה (id: 003598000000000)

לָמָּה
======

לָמָּה (H4100) — לָמָה

inter · לְ · מַה

Perceptive Referents

why?, for what purpose? \= a reference to the cause, reason or purpose of an event; normally used in questions with the purpose of identifying that cause, reason, or purpose; sometimes used in rhetorical questions expressing one's conviction that these things cannot be identified

## לִמּוּד (id: 003600000000000)

לִמּוּד
=======

noun m · למד

Know

accustomed \= state in which animals have adapted themselves to the conditions of a certain environment

[JER 2:24](https://ref.ly/Jer2:24)

Know

accustomed, practiced, schooled \= state in which humans have acquired knowledge or a skill from an identified or unidentified source, ► which usually results in a specific behavior or skill

pupil, disciple \= person who receives instruction from someone else for a relatively long period

verb · לַעַג · לָעֵג

Revile

to mock only used in poetry; \= action by which humans or deities express their disdain of others with words, sounds and/or gestures

[2KI 19:21](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:21) · [2CH 30:10](https://ref.ly/2Chr30:10) · [NEH 2:19](https://ref.ly/Neh2:19) · [NEH 3:33](https://ref.ly/Neh3:33) · [JOB 9:23](https://ref.ly/Job9:23) · [JOB 11:3](https://ref.ly/Job11:3) · [JOB 21:3](https://ref.ly/Job21:3) · [JOB 22:19](https://ref.ly/Job22:19) · [PSA 2:4](https://ref.ly/Ps2:4) · [PSA 22:8](https://ref.ly/Ps22:8) · [PSA 59:9](https://ref.ly/Ps59:9) · [PSA 80:7](https://ref.ly/Ps80:7) · [PRO 1:26](https://ref.ly/Prov1:26) · [PRO 17:5](https://ref.ly/Prov17:5) · [PRO 30:17](https://ref.ly/Prov30:17) · [ISA 37:22](https://ref.ly/Isa37:22) · [JER 20:7](https://ref.ly/Jer20:7)

Speak

**Collocation:** לעג לָשֹׁון

a mocking tongue literally: a mocking tongue; hence: \= action by which humans speak a foreign language that is unintelligible and sounds as if they are mocking

[ISA 33:19](https://ref.ly/Isa33:19)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** 2 Kings 19:21; 2 Chronicles 30:10; Nehemiah 2:19; Nehemiah 3:33; Job 9:23; Job 11:3; Job 21:3; Job 22:19; Psalms 2:4; Psalms 22:8; Psalms 59:9; Psalms 80:7; Proverbs 1:26; Proverbs 17:5; Proverbs 30:17; Isaiah 37:22; Jeremiah 20:7; Isaiah 33:19

לָעֵג

noun m · לעג

People

scoffer only used in poetry; \= humans who express their disdain of others with words, sounds and/or gestures

Hard

Chastise · Relief

**Collocation:** לקח נָקָם · לקח נְקָמָה

to take revenge \= action in which humans or deities harm (other) humans in return for an injury or wrong, and so find relief from their anger

Dead

**Collocation:** לקח נֶפֶשׁ

to take (someone's) life, to kill literally: to take a life; hence: \= causative action by which humans take the life of someone else

[1SA 24:12](https://ref.ly/1Sam24:12) · [1KI 19:4](https://ref.ly/1Kgs19:4) · [1KI 19:10](https://ref.ly/1Kgs19:10) · [1KI 19:14](https://ref.ly/1Kgs19:14) · [PSA 31:14](https://ref.ly/Ps31:14) · [PRO 1:19](https://ref.ly/Prov1:19) · [PRO 11:30](https://ref.ly/Prov11:30)2 · [EZK 33:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek33:6) · [JON 4:3](https://ref.ly/Jonah4:3)

Detach

to take out, to extract literally: to take (something from something else); hence: \= causative action by which humans remove objects that are embedded in other objects

[JOB 28:2](https://ref.ly/Job28:2) · [EZK 15:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek15:3) · [EZK 15:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek15:3)

Dissociate

to take (something) out of (something else) literally: to take (a nation) out of (a larger group); hence: \= causative action by which a deity forms a nation by selecting people from a larger group

[DEU 4:34](https://ref.ly/Deut4:34)

Exist

to take from literally: to take (someone) out of (something else); \= causative action by which God creates a human body out of something else

[GEN 2:23](https://ref.ly/Gen2:23) · [GEN 3:19](https://ref.ly/Gen3:19) · [GEN 3:23](https://ref.ly/Gen3:23)

Engage

to receive, to gain, to undergo, to suffer literally: to receive (an event); hence: \= process by which humans become involved in a certain event

Ingest

to receive, to ingest, to soak up literally: to take (food); hence: \= action by which humans ingest food; ≈ used figuratively for soil soaking up blood

[GEN 4:11](https://ref.ly/Gen4:11)

Move

to remove, to take away literally: to take; hence: \= causative action by which humans, deities, or events take objects or people from a specified location and bring them somewhere else

End

to take away (a situation), to withdraw literally: to take away (a situation from someone); hence: \= causative action by which humans, deities, or forces bring a certain situation to an end

Non\-Exist

to take away literally: to take (something) away; hence: \= causative action by which deities cause objects to disappear from existence

## לֶקַח (id: 003620000000000)

לֶקַח
=====

לֶקַח (H3948)

noun m · לקח

Know

teaching \= causative action by which humans and deities give verbal instruction to other humans, and by which the focus is on the communication of the message rather than the content of the message; ≈ often connoting persuasive or eloquent speech

[DEU 32:2](https://ref.ly/Deut32:2) · [JOB 11:4](https://ref.ly/Job11:4) · [PRO 1:5](https://ref.ly/Prov1:5) · [PRO 4:2](https://ref.ly/Prov4:2) · [PRO 7:21](https://ref.ly/Prov7:21) · [PRO 9:9](https://ref.ly/Prov9:9) · [PRO 16:21](https://ref.ly/Prov16:21) · [PRO 16:23](https://ref.ly/Prov16:23) · [ISA 29:24](https://ref.ly/Isa29:24)

Wendy L. Widder

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 32:2; Job 11:4; Proverbs 1:5; Proverbs 4:2; Proverbs 7:21; Proverbs 9:9; Proverbs 16:21; Proverbs 16:23; Isaiah 29:24

## לקט (id: 003622000000000)

לקט
===

לקט (H3950)

verb · יַלְקוּט · לֶקֶט

Gather

to gather, to glean \= causative action by which humans or animals bring together and take in objects from scattered places or sources

[GEN 31:46](https://ref.ly/Gen31:46) · [GEN 47:14](https://ref.ly/Gen47:14) · [EXO 16:4](https://ref.ly/Exod16:4) · [EXO 16:5](https://ref.ly/Exod16:5) · [EXO 16:16](https://ref.ly/Exod16:16) · [EXO 16:17](https://ref.ly/Exod16:17) · [EXO 16:18](https://ref.ly/Exod16:18) · [EXO 16:21](https://ref.ly/Exod16:21) · [EXO 16:22](https://ref.ly/Exod16:22) · [EXO 16:26](https://ref.ly/Exod16:26) · [EXO 16:27](https://ref.ly/Exod16:27) · [LEV 19:9](https://ref.ly/Lev19:9) · [LEV 19:10](https://ref.ly/Lev19:10) · [LEV 23:22](https://ref.ly/Lev23:22) · [NUM 11:8](https://ref.ly/Num11:8) · [JDG 1:7](https://ref.ly/Judg1:7) · [RUT 2:2](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:2) · [RUT 2:3](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:3) · [RUT 2:7](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:7) · [RUT 2:8](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:8) · [RUT 2:15](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:15) · [RUT 2:15](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:15) · [RUT 2:16](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:16) · [RUT 2:17](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:17) · [RUT 2:17](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:17) · [RUT 2:18](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:18) · [RUT 2:19](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:19) · [RUT 2:23](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:23) · [1SA 20:38](https://ref.ly/1Sam20:38) · [2KI 4:39](https://ref.ly/2Kgs4:39) · [2KI 4:39](https://ref.ly/2Kgs4:39) · [PSA 104:28](https://ref.ly/Ps104:28) · [SNG 6:2](https://ref.ly/Song6:2) · [ISA 17:5](https://ref.ly/Isa17:5) · [ISA 27:12](https://ref.ly/Isa27:12) · [JER 7:18](https://ref.ly/Jer7:18)

Gather

to gather \= process by which humans come together from different places and form a group for a common purpose, such as for a meeting or for war

[JDG 11:3](https://ref.ly/Judg11:3)

Reinier de Blois
